  var consoleTimeStamp =
    window.console && typeof window.console.timeStamp === 'function'
      ? window.console.timeStamp.bind(window.console)
      : null;
  var event = document.createEvent('Event');
  event.initEvent('onUX3Call', true, true);
  var currentPageMarks = {},
  latestMark = {},
  firstMark = 'navigationStart',
  addMark = function(mark) {
    window.performance.mark(mark);
  };
  addEvent = function() {
    if(event && document) {
      document.dispatchEvent(event);
    }
  }
  instrumentation.clearMeasures = function(){
    window.performance.clearMeasures();
  }
  instrumentation.validateZoneMeasure = function(zoneName) {
    var zoneMarksLength = currentPageMarks['PageViewMarks'][zoneName].length +
                            currentPageMarks['ConditionalMarksFlag'][zoneName].length
    if (zoneMarksLength === 0 && latestMark[zoneName]) {
      if(zoneName === 'ux-primary-action-available'){
        addEvent();
      }
      window.performance.measure(zoneName, firstMark, latestMark[zoneName]);
    }
  };
  instrumentation.addPerfMarkForZones = function(zoneName, markName) {
    try {
      /* Check if predefined marks array is available */
      if (
        currentPageMarks['PageViewMarks'][zoneName] &&
        currentPageMarks['PageViewMarks'][zoneName].indexOf(markName) > -1
      ) {
        var markIndex = currentPageMarks['PageViewMarks'][zoneName].indexOf(markName);
        /* Since mark is available in array add the mark and remove it from array */
        addMark(markName);
        latestMark[zoneName] = markName; // keep a copy of the last mark
        if (consoleTimeStamp) {
          consoleTimeStamp(zoneName + '_' + markName); // To capture marks in timeline view
        }
        currentPageMarks['PageViewMarks'][zoneName].splice(markIndex, 1);
        /* Check if mark's array is empty. If empty all marks have been added for a zone and add a measure for that*/
        instrumentation.validateZoneMeasure(zoneName);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      if (window.console) {
        window.console.log('Correct mpulse zone configuration required.', err);
      }
    }
  };
  // Set the initial Page source as server
  instrumentation.pageSource = 'server';
  //  set 1st mark when navigating within the SPA from one route to another
  //  measure will be calculated w.r.t this mark
  instrumentation.setFirstMark = function(fMark) {
    if (typeof fMark === 'string') {
      addMark(fMark);
      firstMark = fMark;
    }
  };
  instrumentation.setPageMarks = function(cPageMarks) {
    if (typeof cPageMarks === 'object') {
      if (Object.keys(currentPageMarks).length > 0) {
        var cPageViewMarks = cPageMarks.PageViewMarks;
        currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-destination-verified'] && (currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-destination-verified'] = currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-destination-verified'].concat(cPageViewMarks['ux-destination-verified']));
        currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-content-displayed'] && (currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-content-displayed'] = currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-content-displayed'].concat(cPageViewMarks['ux-primary-content-displayed']));
        currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-action-available'] && (currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-action-available'] = currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-primary-action-available'].concat(cPageViewMarks['ux-primary-action-available']));
        currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-secondary-content-displayed'] && (currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-secondary-content-displayed'] = currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks['ux-secondary-content-displayed'].concat(cPageViewMarks['ux-secondary-content-displayed']));
        if(cPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag) {
          instrumentation.setConditionalMarksFlag(cPageMarks);
        }
      } else {
        currentPageMarks = cPageMarks;
      }
    }
  };
  instrumentation.setConditionalMarksFlag = function(cPageMarks) {
    if (typeof cPageMarks === 'object') {
      if (Object.keys(currentPageMarks).length > 0) {
        var cConditionalMarksFlag = cPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag;
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-destination-verified'] && (currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-destination-verified'] = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-destination-verified'].concat(cConditionalMarksFlag['ux-destination-verified']));
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-content-displayed'] && (currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-content-displayed'] = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-content-displayed'].concat(cConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-content-displayed']));
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-action-available'] && (currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-action-available'] = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-action-available'].concat(cConditionalMarksFlag['ux-primary-action-available']));
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-secondary-content-displayed'] && (currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-secondary-content-displayed'] = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag['ux-secondary-content-displayed'].concat(cConditionalMarksFlag['ux-secondary-content-displayed']));
      }
    }
  }
  instrumentation.populateConditionallyExpectedMarks = function (zoneName, dynamicContentFlag, dynamicMarksList) {
    var flagIndex;
    /* Remove the flag */
    try {
      flagIndex = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag[zoneName].indexOf(dynamicContentFlag);
      if (flagIndex > -1) {
        /* Check if more than one and different marks exist for a zone based on the same call and add to zone*/
        if (dynamicMarksList && dynamicMarksList.length > 0) {
            currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks[zoneName] = currentPageMarks.PageViewMarks[zoneName].concat(dynamicMarksList);
        }
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag[zoneName].splice(flagIndex, 1);
        /* Check the marks and add measure */
        instrumentation.validateZoneMeasure(zoneName);
      }
    } catch(err) {
      if (window.console) {
        window.console.log('Correct mpulse zone configuration required.', err);
      }
    }
  };
  instrumentation.removeConditionalMarksFlag =  function (zoneName, conditionalMarkFlag) {
    var flagIndex;
    /* Remove the flag */
    try {
      flagIndex = currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag[zoneName].indexOf(conditionalMarkFlag);
      if (flagIndex > -1) {
        currentPageMarks.ConditionalMarksFlag[zoneName].splice(flagIndex, 1);
        /* Check the marks and add measure */
        instrumentation.validateZoneMeasure(zoneName);
      }
    } catch(err) {
      if (window.console) {
        window.console.log('Correct mpulse zone configuration required.', err);
      }
    }
  };
  instrumentation.resetPageMarks = function() {
    latestMark = {},
    currentPageMarks["PageViewMarks"] = {
      'ux-destination-verified': [],
      'ux-primary-content-displayed': [],
      'ux-primary-action-available': [],
      'ux-secondary-content-displayed': [],
    },
    currentPageMarks["ConditionalMarksFlag"] = {
      'ux-destination-verified': [],
      'ux-primary-content-displayed': [],
      'ux-primary-action-available': [],
      'ux-secondary-content-displayed': [],
    }
  };
  instrumentation.getPageMarks = function(){
    return currentPageMarks;
  };
  instrumentation.getPerformanceMeasures = function(type) {
    if (window.performance && window.performance.mark && window.performance.measure) {
      var perfEntries = performance.getEntriesByType(type),
          logText;
      for (var i = 0; i < perfEntries.length; i++) {
        if (perfEntries[i].name.indexOf('ux') < 0) {
          continue;
        }
        logText = "Name: " + perfEntries[i].name +
                        " Entry Type: " + perfEntries[i].entryType +
                        " Start Time: " + perfEntries[i].startTime;
        if (type == "mark") {
                        logText += " | ";
        } else {
                        logText += " Duration: " + perfEntries[i].duration + " | ";
        }
        if (window.console) {
            window.console.log(logText);
        }
      }
    }
  };
  instrumentation.getAllPerfMarks = function () {
    window.instrumentation.getPerformanceMeasures('mark');
  };
  instrumentation.getAllPerfMeasures = function () {
    window.instrumentation.getPerformanceMeasures('measure');
  };
  window.instrumentation = instrumentation;
  //get the siteconfig for page -- mandatory for pages where marks is required
  window.instrumentation.setPageMarks({
      "PageViewMarks":{"ux-destination-verified":["ux-image-inline-logo"],"ux-primary-content-displayed":[],"ux-primary-action-available":[],"ux-secondary-content-displayed":[]},
      "ConditionalMarksFlag":{"ux-destination-verified":["ux-action-before-load"],"ux-primary-content-displayed":["ux-action-before-content-load"],"ux-primary-action-available":[],"ux-secondary-content-displayed":[]}});
    
})();
function instrumentingLoadingMark(measureIdentifier, markIdentifier) {
  if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.instrumentation)
  {
    window.instrumentation.addPerfMarkForZones(
      measureIdentifier,
      markIdentifier
    );
  }
}
